3293:async def run_one_query(
3294:    q: dict,
3295:    out_root: Path,
3296:    *,
3297:    four_role_transport=None,
3298:    four_role_inputs=None,
3299:    four_role_input_builder=None,
3300:    query_index: int | None = None,
3301:    query_total: int | None = None,
3302:    resume: bool = False,
3303:) -> dict:
3304:    """Run the full honest pipeline on one query. Returns a summary dict.
3305:
3306:    I-meta-002 sub-PR-6 (4-role wiring, GUARDED + default OFF): the 4-role evaluation path
3307:    activates ONLY when BOTH ``four_role_transport`` is supplied (an explicit, INJECTED
3308:    ``RoleTransport`` — there is NO default real transport; live transport is Gate-B after lock
3309:    promotion) AND ``PG_FOUR_ROLE_MODE`` is enabled (env "1"/"true"/"True"). When OFF (the
3310:    default), the legacy evaluator-gate path below is byte-unchanged. ``four_role_inputs`` is the
3311:    caller-supplied ``FourRoleEvaluationInputs`` (claims with EXISTING ids, the canonical
3312:    required-element coverage ledger, and the required-S0 set) — the sweep NEVER synthesizes
3313:    them from the report (that extraction is Gate-B). When the branch fires it delegates entirely
3314:    to ``sweep_integration.run_four_role_seam`` (D8 is the single binding gate) and
3315:    overrides BOTH ``manifest['release_allowed']`` AND ``manifest['status']`` from the D8
3316:    decision, demoting the legacy evaluator_gate to ADVISORY metadata only.
3317:
3318:    I-meta-002 PR-9/M3b (Gate-B wiring): ``four_role_input_builder`` is an OPTIONAL no-argument
3319:    closure (wired by ``scripts/dr_benchmark/run_gate_b.py`` over the native
3320:    ``build_native_gate_b_inputs`` + evidence normalization). When supplied it WINS over a
3321:    static ``four_role_inputs``: it is called AFTER generation to PRODUCE the inputs+audit
3322:    bundle, and the seam writes the per-claim audit map to ``four_role_claim_audit.json`` next
3323:    to the run. The default (both None while the branch is OFF) leaves the legacy path
3324:    byte-unchanged.
3325:    """
3326:    reset_run_cost()
3327:    # FX-09 (I-ready-017): begin a per-RUN, concurrency-ISOLATED judge counter so
3328:    # judge_error_rate's denominator is THIS run's ACTUAL judge invocations, not all
3329:    # verifier-checked sentences (the judge only runs on sentences that pass every
3330:    # mechanical check first → the old denominator diluted the #1071 binding
3331:    # abort_verifier_degraded gate ~2.87x). The counter is a contextvar scope, isolated
3332:    # per OS-thread AND per asyncio Task, so a sibling run sharing the process (the v6
3333:    # Dramatiq worker runs `asyncio.run(run_one_query)` under `--threads 2`) cannot
3334:    # contaminate it. Read directly at the rate computation (no process-global delta).
3335:    try:
3336:        from src.polaris_graph.llm.entailment_judge import (
3337:            begin_run_judge_telemetry as _begin_run_judge_telemetry,
3338:        )
3339:        _run_judge_tel = _begin_run_judge_telemetry()
3340:    except Exception:
3341:        _run_judge_tel = None
3342:    # I-bug-111: reset synthesis-scrub alert + telemetry at run
3343:    # boundary so per-run manifest reflects ONLY this run's
3344:    # synthesis behavior. Without this reset, the sticky alert from
3345:    # query N leaks into query N+1's manifest. Defensive lazy
3346:    # import: tolerate environments where the module isn't loaded.
3347:    try:
3348:        from src.polaris_graph.generator.analyst_synthesis import (
3349:            reset_synthesis_scrub_alert,
3350:            reset_synthesis_telemetry,
3351:        )
3352:        reset_synthesis_scrub_alert()
3353:        reset_synthesis_telemetry()
3354:    except Exception:  # noqa: BLE001 — defensive: alert reset failure must not abort run
3355:        pass
3356:
3357:    # I-pipe-015 (#1240, Codex iter-1 REQUEST_CHANGES): reset the MODULE-GLOBAL token-honesty

8821:            def _hb_claims(done: int, n: int) -> None:

8823:                # SAME lock the parent holds when it clears the flag, so an entered-but-preempted
8824:                # worker callback can NOT land a stale four_role_progress after the parent has cleared
8825:                # the flag and written terminal status (the check-then-write race in iter-1's guard).

8859:            _seam_held_reason = None
8860:            # Manage the executor MANUALLY (NOT `with`): a `with ThreadPoolExecutor` __exit__ calls
8861:            # shutdown(wait=True), which BLOCKS until the wedged worker finishes — defeating the
8862:            # timeout entirely (Codex diff-gate P1). shutdown(wait=False, cancel_futures=True) returns

8876:                # into a held seam_error (Codex diff-gate iter-2 P1). The worker's `finally` already
8877:                # updated the cost holder, so the `finally` below reconciles the full spend before
8878:                # this re-raises.
8879:                raise
8880:            except Exception as _seam_exc:  # noqa: BLE001 - any OTHER seam failure must fail CLOSED
8881:                _seam_held_reason = f"seam_error:{type(_seam_exc).__name__}:{str(_seam_exc)[:120]}"

8883:                # Codex AC1-gate iter-2 P1-1: clear the live flag UNDER _hb_lock so it is mutually
8884:                # exclusive with the worker's check-then-write in _hb_claims. An in-flight callback
8885:                # either completes its write BEFORE this acquires the lock, or is blocked and then sees
8886:                # the cleared flag and returns — so NO four_role_progress write can land after this
8887:                # point. Stops an orphaned post-timeout worker from overwriting the terminal heartbeat
8888:                # or bleeding stale progress into the next query's state/run_status.json.
8889:                with _hb_lock:
8890:                    _seam_hb_live[0] = False
8891:                # NON-BLOCKING shutdown so a wedged worker cannot delay the held manifest (P1).
8892:                _seam_pool.shutdown(wait=False, cancel_futures=True)
8893:                # Budget reconciliation: on the SUCCESS path the worker's `finally` already updated
8894:                # `_seam_cost_holder`, so this write-back is EXACT. On the TIMEOUT path the worker is
8895:                # still running (holder == parent cost -> delta 0), so the in-flight verifier spend is
8896:                # NOT added to the parent cap — an acceptable tradeoff (Codex P2): the run is ABORTING
8897:                # (release HELD), the operator authorized spend, the orphaned worker's cost is bounded

2301:# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
2302:# B5/B7 (DUAL_AGREED_PLAN §B5/B7, operator-locked 2026-06-14) — strict_verify drop
2303:# DISPOSITION classifier + report-body disclosure.
2304:#
2305:# The plan's "FIX THE LIVE SILENT-DROP HOLE": strict_verify silently deletes failing
2306:# sentences. Distinguish two dispositions so the drop is NEVER silent — without ever
2307:# rendering a generator-hallucinated sentence as asserted prose:
2308:#
2309:#   * UN-PROVENANCED HARD DROP — the sentence carried no usable [#ev] provenance (or was
2310:#     content-empty). It is not a grounded claim; it is correctly DROPPED with no body
2311:#     content (only counted). These are hygiene drops.
2312:#   * SUPPORT-FAILED DISCLOSED DROP — the sentence DID carry provenance but failed span /
2313:#     numeric / overlap / entailment verification against its own source. This is the
2314:#     "unsupported/contradicted by source" class. The faithfulness rule is ABSOLUTE: the
2315:#     original (hallucinated/unsupported) sentence text MUST NOT render as a finding. The
2316:#     drop is surfaced as a DISCLOSED COUNT + reason, never as the raw failed sentence.
2317:#
2318:# This is faithfulness-NEUTRAL: no failed sentence is resurrected, no asserted prose is
2319:# added. It only converts a silent deletion into a counted, reasoned disclosure.
2320:# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
2321:
2322:# Reasons where the sentence had NO grounded claim to begin with -> hard hygiene drop.

2324:    "no_provenance_token",
2325:    "empty_or_contentless_sentence",
2326:})
2327:
2328:DROP_DISPOSITION_UNPROVENANCED = "unprovenanced_hard_drop"
2329:DROP_DISPOSITION_SUPPORT_FAILED = "support_failed_disclosed"

2331:
2332:def classify_drop_disposition(sv: SentenceVerification) -> str:
2333:    """Classify a strict_verify-dropped ``SentenceVerification`` (B5/B7).
2334:
2335:    Returns ``DROP_DISPOSITION_UNPROVENANCED`` when the sentence had no usable provenance
2336:    (``no_provenance_token`` / ``empty_or_contentless_sentence``) — a hygiene drop with no
2337:    grounded claim. Returns ``DROP_DISPOSITION_SUPPORT_FAILED`` for EVERY other failure
2338:    reason (numeric_mismatch / overlap_too_low / entailment_failed / invalid_token /
2339:    span_out_of_range / calc_* / judge-error fail-closed): the sentence cited provenance but
2340:    failed verification against its own source — the "unsupported/contradicted by source"
2341:    class that must be DISCLOSED (count) but NEVER rendered as asserted prose.
2342:
2343:    Fail-safe: a sentence with NO failure_reasons but is_verified=False is treated as
2344:    support-failed (the stricter, disclosed bucket) — it is never silently nothing.
2345:    """
2346:    reasons = list(getattr(sv, "failure_reasons", None) or [])
2347:    # A dropped sentence is UN-provenanced only if EVERY reason is an unprovenanced reason
2348:    # (and there is at least one). Any support-grounding failure -> the disclosed bucket.
2349:    if reasons and all(r.split(":", 1)[0] in _UNPROVENANCED_DROP_REASONS for r in reasons):
2350:        return DROP_DISPOSITION_UNPROVENANCED
2351:    return DROP_DISPOSITION_SUPPORT_FAILED

2353:
2354:def build_drop_disclosure(dropped_sentences: list[SentenceVerification]) -> dict:
2355:    """Summarize strict_verify drops into a DISCLOSURE record (B5/B7) — counts + reasons only.
2356:
2357:    NEVER includes the raw dropped sentence text (a support-failed sentence is
2358:    generator-hallucinated / unsupported and must not ship as prose). Returns a dict:
2359:    ``{support_failed_count, unprovenanced_count, support_failed_reason_counts,
2360:    unprovenanced_reason_counts}``. Reason counts are SPLIT BY DISPOSITION (Codex diff-gate P2) so
2361:    the support-failed disclosure's reasons match its claim count exactly and are never conflated
2362:    with hygiene (un-provenanced) reasons. Reason keys collapse parameterized detail
2363:    (``reason:detail`` -> ``reason``). Both reason maps are empty when there are no drops of that
2364:    disposition.
2365:    """
2366:    support_failed = 0
2367:    unprovenanced = 0
2368:    support_failed_reason_counts: dict[str, int] = {}
2550:    stripped = _PLACEBO_COMPARATOR_RE.sub(" ", stripped)
2551:    stripped = _THRESHOLD_RE.sub(" ", stripped)
2552:    no_content = not _content_words(stripped)
2553:    no_numbers = not _decimals_in(stripped) and not _numbers_in(stripped)
2554:    return no_content and no_numbers

 succeeded in 473ms:
1:"""I-arch-005 B14 (#1257) — shared SIDE-JUDGE empty-content guard + retry + IO trace.
2:
3:A *side judge* is any non-binding evaluator LLM call that is NOT one of the four locked
4:faithfulness roles (e.g. the cross-document NLI conflict judge, the credibility judge,
5:the entailment side-judge). Their shared failure mode (forensically observed mid-run on
6:drb_72 / drb_75, 2026-06-12..14) is the **empty-content collapse**: a reasoning model
7:(GLM-5.1) burns its whole token budget on hidden reasoning and returns a 200 with an
8:EMPTY / None / whitespace ``message.content``. Downstream that becomes ``json.loads(None)``
9:(a ``TypeError``) → a broad ``except`` → either a silent fail-open ('neutral', 0.0) that
10:DROPS a possible real finding, or a fail-CLOSED raise that HOLDS the whole report.
11:
12:This module is the ONE place that:
13:  (a) detects empty/None/whitespace content (``is_empty_content``);
14:  (b) RETRIES the call on empty content (inheriting the proven 4-role transport retry
15:      posture — see ``semantic_conflict_detector`` empty-content note + the existing
16:      retries; here the retry is a fresh re-invocation of the injected call);
17:  (c) captures the raw request/response of EVERY attempt to a trace (and, when a
18:      run-scoped raw-IO sink is active, to ``<run_dir>/llm_io/`` — the empty-content
19:      upstream cause is currently INFERENCE; this capture exists to CONFIRM it);
20:  (d) on persistent empty returns a typed ``JudgeUnavailable`` sentinel — it NEVER
21:      raises. "VERIFY = LABEL, NEVER HOLD" (operator-locked 2026-06-14): a side-judge
22:      infra failure may only ADD a disclosed label, never prevent artifact emission.
23:
24:POSTURE (binding):
25:  * PURE-ADDITIVE. No production caller is changed by importing this module; callers opt
26:    in. It NEVER widens a span, never flips ``is_verified``, never makes a failing claim
27:    pass — it only converts an empty-content judge failure into a disclosed *label*.
28:  * The LLM call is DEPENDENCY-INJECTED (``call_fn``) so the guard is fully offline-
29:    testable with a deterministic fake (no network, no model, no spend).
30:  * NEVER raises for an empty/None result. It DOES re-raise a caller-designated
31:    "propagate" exception class (e.g. ``BudgetExceededError``) unchanged — a budget cap
32:    breach is a clean stop signal, not an unadjudicated side-judge call.
33:  * LAW VI: the retry count is an env-overridable named constant (no magic number).
34:"""
35:from __future__ import annotations
36:
37:import logging
38:import os

40:from dataclasses import dataclass, field
41:from typing import Any, Callable
42:
43:logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
44:
45:# LAW VI — env-overridable retry budget. Default 2 retries (3 total attempts): the
46:# empty-content collapse is intermittent (a single provider hiccup), so a small bounded
47:# retry recovers the common case without inflating spend. 0 => one attempt, no retry.
48:_ENV_RETRIES = "PG_SIDE_JUDGE_EMPTY_RETRIES"
49:_DEFAULT_RETRIES = 2
50:
51:
52:def side_judge_empty_retries() -> int:
53:    """Resolve the empty-content retry budget (LAW VI). Non-int / negative => default."""
54:    try:
55:        n = int(os.environ.get(_ENV_RETRIES, "") or _DEFAULT_RETRIES)
56:    except (TypeError, ValueError):
57:        return _DEFAULT_RETRIES
58:    return n if n >= 0 else _DEFAULT_RETRIES
59:
60:
61:def is_empty_content(content: Any) -> bool:
62:    """True iff ``content`` is None / not a string / empty / whitespace-only.
63:
64:    This is the exact predicate the downstream ``json.loads(content)`` chokes on:
65:    ``json.loads(None)`` raises ``TypeError`` and ``json.loads("")`` /
66:    ``json.loads("   ")`` raise ``json.JSONDecodeError`` — every one is an
67:    empty-content collapse, not a real verdict. Kept total (never raises) so it is
68:    safe to call on any raw provider payload.
69:    """
70:    if content is None:
71:        return True
72:    if not isinstance(content, str):
73:        return True
74:    return content.strip() == ""

77:@dataclass
78:class JudgeUnavailable:
79:    """Typed sentinel: the side judge could not produce non-empty content after retries.
80:
81:    This is a *value*, not an exception — the whole point (operator-locked 2026-06-14):
82:    a side-judge infra failure must be LABELABLE, never raisable into a report HOLD. The
83:    caller converts this into a disclosed gap label (e.g. ``conflict_unscored`` /
84:    ``credibility_unscored``); it asserts NOTHING about the underlying claim — only that
85:    the judge could not adjudicate.
86:
87:    ``attempts`` is the number of calls made; ``reason`` is a short human string;
88:    ``last_response`` is the final raw provider payload (for the forensic trace).
89:    """
90:
91:    reason: str
92:    attempts: int = 0
93:    last_response: Any = None
94:
95:
96:@dataclass
97:class SideJudgeAttempt:
98:    """One captured request/response attempt (the in-memory forensic trace row)."""
99:
100:    call_id: str
101:    attempt: int
102:    request: Any
103:    raw_response: Any
104:    empty: bool

107:@dataclass
108:class SideJudgeOutcome:
109:    """The guard result: either a parsed ``value`` or a ``JudgeUnavailable`` sentinel.
110:
111:    ``value`` is the injected ``call_fn``'s return on the FIRST non-empty attempt (the
112:    caller parses it). ``unavailable`` is set iff every attempt returned empty content.
113:    ``trace`` is the list of every attempt's captured request/response (always present
114:    so a test can assert raw IO was captured even on the success path).
115:    """
116:
117:    value: Any = None
118:    unavailable: JudgeUnavailable | None = None
119:    trace: list = field(default_factory=list)
120:
121:    @property
122:    def is_unavailable(self) -> bool:
123:        return self.unavailable is not None
124:
125:
126:def call_side_judge_with_guard(
127:    call_fn: Callable[[], Any],
128:    *,
129:    extract_content: Callable[[Any], Any],
130:    call_type: str,
131:    role: str | None = None,
132:    build_request: Callable[[], Any] | None = None,
133:    propagate: tuple = (),
134:    retries: int | None = None,
135:    io_sink: Any = None,
136:) -> SideJudgeOutcome:
137:    """Call a side judge with empty-content retry + raw-IO capture + a no-raise sentinel.
138:
139:    Parameters
140:    ----------
141:    call_fn:
142:        Zero-arg callable that performs ONE side-judge LLM call and returns its RAW
143:        provider response (the thing ``extract_content`` reads). Injected so the guard is
144:        offline-testable. May raise a ``propagate`` exception (re-raised unchanged) — any
145:        OTHER exception is captured as an empty/failed attempt (NEVER re-raised).
146:    extract_content:
147:        ``raw_response -> content`` projector (e.g.
148:        ``lambda r: r["choices"][0]["message"]["content"]``). Run under a guard so a
149:        malformed shape counts as empty, not a crash.
150:    call_type / role:
151:        Forensic tags for the raw-IO sink record.
152:    build_request:
153:        Optional zero-arg callable returning the request body to record (for the trace).
154:        Kept lazy so the caller can capture the exact final body per attempt.
155:    propagate:
156:        Exception classes that MUST escape unchanged (e.g. ``BudgetExceededError``).
157:    retries:
158:        Override the env retry budget (tests). ``None`` => ``side_judge_empty_retries()``.
159:    io_sink:
160:        Optional run-scoped raw-IO sink (``LlmIoSink``). ``None`` => only the active
161:        ambient sink (``openrouter_client.current_raw_io_sink()``) is used, if any.
162:
163:    Returns
164:    -------
165:    SideJudgeOutcome with EITHER ``value`` (first non-empty response) OR ``unavailable``
166:    (a ``JudgeUnavailable`` after all attempts returned empty). Never raises except for a
167:    ``propagate`` class.
168:    """
169:    n_retries = side_judge_empty_retries() if retries is None else max(0, int(retries))

171:    trace: list = []

173:
174:    sink = io_sink
175:    if sink is None:
176:        try:
177:            from src.polaris_graph.llm import openrouter_client as _orc  # noqa: PLC0415
178:            sink = _orc.current_raw_io_sink()
179:        except Exception:  # noqa: BLE001 — sink discovery must never break the call
180:            sink = None

182:    for attempt in range(1, total_attempts + 1):
183:        request_body: Any = None
184:        if build_request is not None:
185:            try:
186:                request_body = build_request()
187:            except Exception:  # noqa: BLE001 — request capture must never break the call
188:                request_body = None

190:        empty = True

192:        try:
193:            raw_response = call_fn()

195:            raise
196:        except Exception as exc:  # noqa: BLE001 — a transport/parse failure is an empty attempt
197:            logger.warning(

199:                call_type, attempt, total_attempts, exc,
200:            )
201:            raw_response = {"error": str(exc)}
202:            empty = True
203:        else:
204:            try:
205:                content = extract_content(raw_response)
206:            except Exception:  # noqa: BLE001 — malformed shape == empty content
207:                content = None
208:            empty = is_empty_content(content)
209:        last_response = raw_response
210:
211:        # Capture EVERY attempt's request/response — empty or not — to the forensic trace
212:        # (and the run-scoped raw-IO sink when active). The empty-content upstream cause is
213:        # currently INFERENCE; this capture is how we CONFIRM it. Best-effort, never raises.
214:        trace.append(SideJudgeAttempt(
215:            call_id=call_id, attempt=attempt, request=request_body,
216:            raw_response=raw_response, empty=empty,
217:        ))
218:        if sink is not None:
219:            try:
220:                sink.record(
221:                    call_id=call_id,
222:                    call_type=call_type,
223:                    role=role,
224:                    request=request_body,
225:                    raw_response=raw_response,
226:                    duration_ms=None,
227:                    status=("ok" if not empty else "empty_content"),
228:                )
229:            except Exception:  # noqa: BLE001 — capture must never perturb the call
230:                pass
231:
232:        if not empty:
233:            return SideJudgeOutcome(value=raw_response, unavailable=None, trace=trace)
234:
235:    # Every attempt returned empty content → a typed sentinel, NEVER a raise.
236:    logger.warning(
237:        "[side-judge:%s] persistent empty content after %d attempt(s) -> JudgeUnavailable "
238:        "(LABEL, never HOLD)", call_type, total_attempts,
239:    )
240:    return SideJudgeOutcome(
241:        value=None,
242:        unavailable=JudgeUnavailable(
243:            reason=f"{call_type}: empty content after {total_attempts} attempt(s)",
244:            attempts=total_attempts,
245:            last_response=last_response,

405:
406:def _run_chain(
407:    research_question: str,
408:    rows: list[dict],
409:    *,
410:    gov_suffixes: tuple,
411:    domain: str | None,
412:    judge: Callable | None,
413:    now_year: int | None,
414:) -> CredibilityAnalysis:
415:    """The P4→P3→P2→P5→P6 chain body; wrapped by run_credibility_analysis for the fail-loud posture."""
416:    # ── P4: independent-origin collapse → per-row assignment, on COPIED rows (never mutate the caller) ──
417:    collapse = collapse_independent_origins(rows, gov_suffixes=gov_suffixes)
418:    if len(collapse.assignments) != len(rows):
419:        raise CredibilityPassError(
420:            "abort_independence_annotation_gap: P4 returned "
421:            f"{len(collapse.assignments)} assignments for {len(rows)} rows"
422:        )
423:    annotated: list[dict] = []
424:    origin_by_evidence: dict = {}
425:    for i, row in enumerate(rows):
426:        eid = _require_evidence_id(row, i)
427:        assignment = collapse.assignments[i]
428:        new_row = dict(row)  # COPY
429:        new_row["origin_cluster_id"] = assignment.origin_cluster_id
430:        new_row["is_canonical_origin"] = assignment.is_canonical_origin
431:        annotated.append(new_row)
432:        origin_by_evidence[eid] = assignment.origin_cluster_id
433:
434:    # ── P3: supersession multiplier per source ──
435:    supers_by_evidence = {
436:        _require_evidence_id(row, i): supersession_adjustment(row, now_year=now_year)
437:        for i, row in enumerate(annotated)
438:    }
439:
440:    # ── P2: credibility judgments — judge_error / judge=None LABEL the source, never abort ──
441:    # I-arch-005 B12 (#1257, operator-locked 2026-06-14 "VERIFY = LABEL, NEVER HOLD"): the pass
442:    # is ADVISORY (its own docstring). The two INFRA conditions must NOT abort the WHOLE report —
443:    # each LABELS the affected source(s) ``credibility_unscored`` (a disclosed gap) and KEEPS the
444:    # rest scoring with real weights:
445:    #   * a PER-SOURCE judge_error — ``score_source_credibility`` already isolates the error to ONE
446:    #     row and falls back to that source's DETERMINISTIC priors (a real, honest weight, never
447:    #     fabricated), flagging it ``judge_error=True``;
448:    #   * judge=None (no production judge wired) — ``score_source_credibility(judge=None)`` returns
449:    #     priors-only for EVERY row but with ``judge_error=False`` (it is not a per-source error, it
450:    #     is a global infra condition). So the ``errored_ids`` set is EMPTY in that case; we OR in
451:    #     ``judge_missing`` below so EVERY source is correctly labeled ``credibility_unscored`` (NOT a
452:    #     silent priors-only false-green — that EXACT trap is why the explicit OR exists).
453:    # The credibility WEIGHT math is unchanged — a labeled row simply carries its priors-only weight +
454:    # the disclosed label. (The genuine provenance hole — a CITED evidence_id with NO credibility row
455:    # at all — is still fail-loud, caught downstream by ``apply_disclosure_to_svs``'s coverage
456:    # assertion; that is a real coverage gap, NOT a recoverable infra condition.)
457:    judge_missing = judge is None
458:    judgments = score_source_credibility(research_question, annotated, domain=domain, judge=judge)
459:    errored_ids = {j.evidence_id for j in judgments if getattr(j, "judge_error", False)}
460:    if errored_ids:
461:        example = sorted(errored_ids)[:5]
462:        # LOUD log (LAW II: no silent downgrade) — the run still ships, but the operator sees it.
463:        import logging as _logging  # noqa: PLC0415
464:        _logging.getLogger(__name__).warning(
465:            "[credibility-pass] credibility judge errored for %d/%d source(s) (e.g. %s); "
466:            "LABELING them credibility_unscored (priors-only weight) and continuing to score the "
467:            "rest — the report ships with the disclosed gap (never aborts the basket).",
468:            len(errored_ids), len(judgments), example,
469:        )
470:
471:    # ── POST-P3 credibility = P2 weight × supersession multiplier (certainty carried, not folded away) ──
472:    credibility_by_evidence: dict = {}
473:    for row, judgment in zip(annotated, judgments):
474:        eid = judgment.evidence_id
475:        supersession = supers_by_evidence.get(eid)
476:        multiplier = supersession.multiplier if supersession else 1.0
477:        credibility_by_evidence[eid] = EvidenceCredibility(
478:            evidence_id=eid,
479:            credibility_weight=_clamp01(judgment.credibility_weight * multiplier),
480:            reliability_score=judgment.reliability_score,
481:            relevance_score=judgment.relevance_score,
482:            origin_cluster_id=origin_by_evidence.get(eid, ""),
483:            is_canonical_origin=bool(row.get("is_canonical_origin")),
484:            certainty_downgrade=bool(supersession.certainty_downgrade) if supersession else False,
485:            soft_warning=(supersession.soft_warning if supersession else None),
486:            # OR in ``judge_missing``: with judge=None EVERY source is priors-only with
487:            # judge_error=False, so ``errored_ids`` is empty — without the OR every source would ship
488:            # credibility_unscored=False (a silent priors-only false-green, the EXACT trap B12-P1 fixes).
489:            credibility_unscored=(eid in errored_ids) or judge_missing,
490:        )
491:
492:    # POST-P3 judgments for downstream — P6 disclosure must use the post-P3 credibility, not raw P2.
493:    adjusted_judgments = [
494:        dataclasses.replace(j, credibility_weight=credibility_by_evidence[j.evidence_id].credibility_weight)
495:        for j in judgments
496:    ]
497:
498:    # ── P5: claim graph (atomic claims + contradiction edges) ──
499:    graph = build_claim_graph(annotated, domain=domain)
500:
501:    # ── P6: origin-cluster weight-mass (mass = authority(canonical) ONLY; credibility disclosed) ──
502:    weight_mass = aggregate_weight_mass(graph.claims, annotated, adjusted_judgments)
503:
504:    # ── I-arch-002 [8] — assemble per-claim baskets with ISOLATED per-member verification.
505:    # The verifier is the PRODUCTION single-sentence callable, lazy-imported here so this

2178:# Attribute / dict-key names the JUDGES lane (B12 credibility-side + B13 conflict-side) attaches
2179:# its PER-SOURCE / PER-PAIR labeled returns under. The JUDGES lane is NOT in this base (8002392e),

2186:def _collect_judge_unscored_labels(multi, retrieval) -> dict:
2187:    """B12/B13 run-side glue (I-arch-005 #1257). DEFENSIVELY collect the JUDGES-lane PER-SOURCE
2188:    (``credibility_unscored``) and PER-PAIR (``conflict_unscored``) labeled returns from whichever
2189:    object the lane attaches them to (the generator result ``multi`` or the ``retrieval`` bundle),
2190:    tolerant of their TOTAL absence at this base (the lane is not integrated yet).
2191:
2192:    Detection is by ATTRIBUTE then dict-KEY name on each candidate carrier; a found value is
2193:    normalized to a list (a scalar/str is wrapped). Returns
2194:    ``{"credibility_unscored": [...], "conflict_unscored": [...]}`` with empty lists when absent.
2195:    Pure read-only; never raises into the run (the caller also guards)."""
2196:    def _read(carrier, name):
2197:        if carrier is None:
2198:            return None
2199:        val = getattr(carrier, name, None)
2200:        if val is None and isinstance(carrier, dict):
2201:            val = carrier.get(name)
2202:        return val
2203:
2204:    def _as_list(val):
2205:        if val is None:
2206:            return []
2207:        if isinstance(val, (list, tuple, set)):
2208:            return [v for v in val if v is not None]
2209:        return [val]
2210:
2211:    out = {_CREDIBILITY_UNSCORED_ATTR: [], _CONFLICT_UNSCORED_ATTR: []}
2212:    for carrier in (multi, retrieval):
2213:        for key in (_CREDIBILITY_UNSCORED_ATTR, _CONFLICT_UNSCORED_ATTR):
2214:            found = _as_list(_read(carrier, key))
2215:            if found:
2216:                out[key].extend(found)
2217:    return out

389:
390:def is_hard_block(
391:    *,
392:    fabricated_occurrence_latched: bool,
393:    zero_verified: bool,
394:    zero_usable_evidence: bool,
395:    redaction_active: bool = True,
396:) -> bool:
397:    """The canonical no-fabrication hard line — narrowed per B5/B7 (operator-ratified 2026-06-14).
398:
399:    A report is HARD-blocked iff there is true zero-grounding (no VERIFIED claim AND no usable
400:    evidence), OR a FABRICATED occurrence latched WHILE per-claim redaction is NOT active.
401:
402:    ``redaction_active`` (default True — production leaves ``PG_REDACT_HELD_UNSUPPORTED`` ON, the
403:    kill-switch is test/offline-only) is the SAFETY COUPLING the narrowing depends on: a fabricated
404:    claim is allowed to ship-minus-itself ONLY because the redactor guarantees the fabricated claim's
405:    prose is excised. If redaction is disabled, the fabricated claim could ship as asserted prose, so
406:    FABRICATED REMAINS a hard block — the narrowing is gated on the excision being guaranteed.
407:    Zero-grounding is ALWAYS a hard block regardless of redaction.
408:    """
409:    if zero_verified and zero_usable_evidence:
410:        return True
411:    if fabricated_occurrence_latched and not redaction_active:
412:        return True
413:    return False

416:@dataclass
417:class ReleaseOutcome:
418:    """The always-release-aware release outcome over a D8 ``ReleaseDecision`` (I-perm-001).
419:
420:    ``released`` — a report ships (normal OR honest-insufficient-safety variant).
421:    ``hard_block`` — the no-fabrication hard line fired; NO report ships as clean.
422:    ``normal_release_blocked`` — the polished normal report is withheld (hard_block OR the clinical
423:        safety floor is insufficient), but an honest report may still ship.
424:    ``status`` — the terminal pipeline status.
425:    ``disclosed_gaps`` — the held reasons surfaced as DISPLAYED labels (not blockers).
426:    ``release_quality_score`` — the displayed coverage fraction (NOT a trap-door threshold).
427:    """
428:
429:    released: bool
430:    hard_block: bool
431:    normal_release_blocked: bool
432:    status: str
433:    disclosed_gaps: list[str]
434:    hard_block_reasons: list[str]
435:    release_quality_score: float
436:    safety_floor: str  # "ok" | "insufficient"

439:def always_release_enabled() -> bool:
440:    """PG_ALWAYS_RELEASE — production DEFAULT ON (B5/B7: "nothing shall hold the report").
441:
442:    OFF only on an EXPLICIT off token ('0'/'false'/'no'/'off'). Unset, EMPTY (''), OR any
443:    unrecognized value resolves to the default (ON) — a default-ON flag must never SILENTLY
444:    withhold a report on an unset/empty/typo value. The OFF switch is the byte-identical
445:    legacy-regression escape hatch; legacy callers pass it explicitly ('0' via env, or
446:    always_release=False to compute_release_outcome) and never as an empty string.
447:    """
448:    import os
449:
450:    return os.environ.get(_ENV_ALWAYS_RELEASE, "").strip().lower() not in _OFF_VALUES

129:def _credibility_guard_decision(
130:    *, judge: Any, gov_suffixes: Any, always_release: bool,
131:) -> str:
132:    """I-arch-005 B12-COMPLETION (#1257): the PURE decision for the credibility-pass
133:    pre-run guard, extracted so it is directly unit-testable (the inline guard runs deep in
134:    ``generate_multi_section_report`` after the LLM outline/section calls).
135:
136:    Returns:
137:      * ``"run"`` — judge + gov_suffixes ARE threaded; run the pass normally.
138:      * ``"degrade"`` — judge missing / gov_suffixes missing AND always-release ON; degrade
139:        to the credibility-OFF path (credibility_analysis stays None) + a disclosed gap +
140:        CONTINUE. The caller MUST NOT run the pass body with a None judge.
141:      * ``"raise"`` — judge missing / gov_suffixes missing AND always-release OFF (legacy);
142:        the caller raises CredibilityPassError fail-closed (byte-identical to pre-fix).
143:
144:    This is the keystone of B12-COMPLETION: pre-fix the raise fired BEFORE the B5/B7
145:    always-release try, so judge=None HELD the whole report even under always-release. Now
146:    the decision is gated on always_release so "label not hold" is live in production."""
147:    if judge is None or not gov_suffixes:
148:        return "degrade" if always_release else "raise"
149:    return "run"

1834:    run body produces PERMANENT silence — a `finally` cannot fire on a hang — so the
1835:    call site wraps the whole `run_one_query` in `asyncio.wait_for(..., this)` and
1836:    the B11 finalizer emits a labeled timeout artifact on TimeoutError.
1837:
1838:    LAW VI: env-overridable (PG_RUN_WALL_CLOCK_SEC); generous default. A non-positive
1839:    or unparseable value falls back to the generous default (never disables the guard
1840:    silently — a disabled wall-clock would re-open the permanent-silence class)."""
1841:    raw = os.environ.get(_RUN_WALL_CLOCK_ENV, "").strip()
1842:    if not raw:
1843:        return _RUN_WALL_CLOCK_DEFAULT_SEC
1844:    try:
1845:        val = float(raw)
1846:    except ValueError:
1847:        logging.getLogger(__name__).warning(
1848:            "%s=%r is not a number; using default %.0fs",
1849:            _RUN_WALL_CLOCK_ENV, raw, _RUN_WALL_CLOCK_DEFAULT_SEC,
1850:        )
1851:        return _RUN_WALL_CLOCK_DEFAULT_SEC
1852:    return val if val > 0 else _RUN_WALL_CLOCK_DEFAULT_SEC

2004:def artifact_kind_for_status(status: "str | None", *, timed_out: bool = False) -> str:
2005:    """B11: choose the human-artifact KIND for a terminal status. ``timed_out`` (B20)
2006:    forces the timeout kind regardless of status. Unknown statuses fall to a generic
2007:    degraded body (loud, never silent). PURE — no faithfulness decision."""
2008:    if timed_out:
2009:        return _ARTIFACT_KIND_TIMEOUT
2010:    if not status:
2011:        return _ARTIFACT_KIND_DEGRADED
2012:    # Map a legacy summary label through unification first if it is not already unified.
2013:    unified = status if status in _STATUS_ARTIFACT_KIND else to_unified_status(status)
2014:    return _STATUS_ARTIFACT_KIND.get(
2015:        unified, _STATUS_ARTIFACT_KIND.get(status, _ARTIFACT_KIND_DEGRADED)
2016:    )

2019:def build_finalizer_artifact_body(
2020:    *,
2021:    research_question: str,
2022:    status: "str | None",
2023:    error: "str | None",
2024:    timed_out: bool = False,
2025:    wall_clock_seconds: "float | None" = None,
2026:) -> str:
2027:    """B11 / B20: build the NAMED backstop human artifact for a run that exited WITHOUT
2028:    writing a report.md (a pre-success abort, an exception, or a HANG). PURE function so
2029:    a behavior test can call it without driving the pipeline.
2030:
2031:    This is the artifact the §-1.1 forensic audit reads when no findings report exists —
2032:    it must be self-documenting (what happened, why, the terminal status), never empty.
2033:    It carries NO claims and asserts NO findings, so it can never relax faithfulness."""
2034:    kind = artifact_kind_for_status(status, timed_out=timed_out)
2035:    heading = _ARTIFACT_KIND_HEADINGS.get(kind, "Pipeline verdict")
2036:    lines = [
2037:        f"# Research report: {research_question}",
2038:        "",
2039:        "## Pipeline verdict",
2040:        "",
2041:        f"**Artifact kind:** {kind}",
2042:        f"**Terminal status:** `{status or 'unknown'}`",
2043:    ]
2044:    if timed_out and wall_clock_seconds is not None:
2045:        lines.append(
2046:            f"**Wall-clock:** the run exceeded the {wall_clock_seconds:.0f}s "
2047:            f"run-level wall-clock ({_RUN_WALL_CLOCK_ENV}) and was terminated. "
2048:            "A hang produces no findings; this artifact is emitted so the run is "
2049:            "never silent."
2050:        )
2051:    lines.append("")
2052:    lines.append(f"### {heading}")
2053:    lines.append("")
2054:    if kind == _ARTIFACT_KIND_TIMEOUT:
2055:        lines.append(
2056:            "The pipeline did not complete within the run-level wall-clock. No "
2057:            "findings report was produced. This is a degraded-run disclosure, not a "
2058:            "findings report — no claim is asserted and none is silently dropped."
2059:        )
2060:    elif kind == _ARTIFACT_KIND_REFUSAL:
2061:        lines.append(
2062:            "The pipeline declined to produce a findings report for this query "
2063:            "(scope / safety / corpus-approval / contract refusal). No findings are "
2064:            "asserted; this is an honest refusal, not a silent failure."
2065:        )
2066:    elif kind == _ARTIFACT_KIND_INSUFFICIENT:
2067:        lines.append(
2068:            "The retrieved evidence was insufficient to ship verified findings "
2069:            "(no sources, inadequate corpus, or no section survived strict_verify). "
2070:            "No unverified claim is shipped; this is an insufficient-evidence "
2071:            "disclosure, not a silent drop."
2072:        )
2073:    elif kind == _ARTIFACT_KIND_DISCLOSED_GAPS:
2074:        lines.append(
2075:            "A judge / verifier signal could not be obtained for part of this run. "
2076:            "The gap is DISCLOSED here rather than silently treated as 'no problem'. "
2077:            "No conflict / finding is asserted and none is silently dropped — the "
2078:            "judge simply could not decide."
2079:        )
2080:    else:  # degraded
2081:        lines.append(
2082:            "The run hit a run-level or infrastructure failure before a findings "
2083:            "report could be assembled. This artifact is emitted so the run is never "
2084:            "silent. No findings are asserted."
2085:        )
2086:    if error:
2087:        lines.append("")
2088:        lines.append("### Detail")
2089:        lines.append("")
2090:        lines.append(f"```\n{str(error)[:1000]}\n```")
2091:    lines.append("")
2092:    lines.append("### Suggested next steps")
2093:    lines.append("")
2094:    lines.append("- Inspect `manifest.json` (terminal status + cost) next to this file.")
2095:    lines.append("- Re-run after addressing the disclosed cause; widen retrieval or "
2096:                 "raise the wall-clock if the run was truncated.")
2097:    lines.append("")
2098:    return "\n".join(lines)

2101:def finalize_run_artifact(
2102:    run_dir: "Path | None",
2103:    summary: dict,
2104:    q: dict,
2105:    *,
2106:    timed_out: bool = False,
2107:    wall_clock_seconds: "float | None" = None,
2108:    log=None,
2109:) -> "str | None":
2110:    """B11 keystone — the Universal Artifact Finalizer. Guarantees EXACTLY ONE non-empty
2111:    human artifact exists in ``run_dir`` on EVERY exit path of a run.
2112:
2113:    Contract:
2114:      * If a NON-EMPTY ``report.md`` already exists (the success path, or any abort path
2115:        that wrote its own verdict body) -> NO-OP. NEVER overwrites a real report.md.
2116:      * Else -> write a NAMED backstop artifact (``report.md``) whose body matches the
2117:        already-computed terminal ``summary['status']`` (or the B20 timeout). The status
2118:        is READ, never decided here.
2119:
2120:    Idempotent + crash-safe: called from the run body's `finally` (catches exceptions /
2121:    pre-success aborts that wrote a manifest only) AND from the call-site timeout handler
2122:    (B20 — a hang the `finally` cannot reach). Whichever fires first wins; the second
2123:    no-ops on the now-present report.md.
2124:
2125:    MUST NEVER RAISE (it runs inside a `finally`): all IO is wrapped. Returns the artifact
2126:    kind written, or None if it no-op'd / could not write.
2127:
2128:    Faithfulness: PURE backstop. It asserts no claim and emits no findings — it can only
2129:    ADD a disclosure artifact, never relax a span / provenance / verdict check."""
2130:    def _emit_log(msg: str) -> None:
2131:        try:
2132:            if log is not None:
2133:                log(msg)
2134:            else:
2135:                logging.getLogger(__name__).info(msg)
2136:        except Exception:  # noqa: BLE001 — logging must never break the finalizer
2137:            pass
2138:
2139:    try:
2140:        if run_dir is None:
2141:            return None
2142:        report_path = Path(run_dir) / "report.md"
2143:        # NEVER overwrite a real (non-empty) report.md — the success path and the
2144:        # self-documenting abort bodies already wrote their artifact.
2145:        try:
2146:            if report_path.is_file() and report_path.stat().st_size > 0:
2147:                return None
2148:        except OSError:
2149:            # stat failed; fall through to a best-effort write (better an artifact
2150:            # than risk silence). A subsequent write replaces only an unreadable/empty file.
2151:            pass
2152:        status = summary.get("status") if isinstance(summary, dict) else None
2153:        error = summary.get("error") if isinstance(summary, dict) else None
2154:        body = build_finalizer_artifact_body(
2155:            research_question=q.get("question", "") if isinstance(q, dict) else "",
2156:            status=status,
2157:            error=error,
2158:            timed_out=timed_out,
2159:            wall_clock_seconds=wall_clock_seconds,
2160:        )
2161:        try:
2162:            Path(run_dir).mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
2163:            report_path.write_text(body, encoding="utf-8")
2164:        except OSError as exc:
2165:            _emit_log(f"[finalizer]   FAILED to write backstop artifact: {exc}")
2166:            return None

 succeeded in 486ms:
1:"""LANE-CI (B23) — status-schema parity gate (I-arch-005 Phase-2/3, umbrella #1257).
2:
3:PURPOSE
4:-------
5:Every terminal status that ``scripts/run_honest_sweep_r3.py`` can write into
6:``manifest.status`` MUST be a known value in the shared *downstream* registries
7:that consume that field. A runner status that is unknown downstream is a real
8:production bug:
9:
10:  * ``PipelineStatus`` (``src/polaris_v6/schemas/run_status.py``) — the v6 actor
11:    loads ``manifest.status`` into ``RunStatusResponse.pipeline_status``. A value
12:    outside the ``Literal`` 500s Pydantic validation on a *real* run, so the UI
13:    cannot render that terminal at all. The in-code comments call this the
14:    contract ("must mirror UNIFIED_STATUS_VALUES or RunStatusResponse 500s").
15:  * ``KNOWN_STATUS_VALUES`` (``src/polaris_graph/audit_ir/regression_lab.py``) —
16:    the regression lab's named status registry (``frozenset(_STATUS_TIERS)``); an
17:    unknown status is silently mis-bucketed.
18:
19:This gate is a **read-only STATIC scan**. It AST-parses ALL THREE source files
20:(the runner producer set + both downstream registries) and imports NOTHING from
21:``src/`` or ``scripts/``. Consequences:
22:  * no pipeline runs, no LLM/network, no heavy retrieval import chain executes;
23:  * the gate cannot ImportError under a minimal CI dependency set — it needs only
24:    the stdlib (``ast``) + pytest. This is deliberate: importing
25:    ``regression_lab`` / the runner would pull the production import chain, the
26:    exact fragility a CI parity gate must not have.
27:
28:PRODUCER SET (what can reach ``manifest.status``)
29:-------------------------------------------------
30:The producer set is recovered TWO complementary ways, both static:
31:
32:  1. The *declared* taxonomy: ``UNIFIED_STATUS_VALUES`` ∪
33:     ``set(_SUMMARY_TO_UNIFIED.values())``. The runner either writes a unified
34:     value directly (``UNIFIED_STATUS_VALUES``) or routes a legacy
35:     ``summary["status"]`` label through ``to_unified_status`` (whose codomain is
36:     exactly the ``_SUMMARY_TO_UNIFIED`` values, defaulting to
37:     ``error_unexpected`` which is itself in the set). The legacy *keys* are not
38:     producers — only the mapped *values* land in the manifest — so the declared
39:     set scans the dict *values*.
40:
41:  2. The *actual emission sites*: a STATIC AST scan of EVERY literal status the
42:     runner emits into status-space. Three syntactic forms produce a
43:     ``manifest.status``, and ALL THREE are scanned (missing any one lets a new
44:     literal escape both the declared-set parity check and this gate):
45:
46:       a. plain-Name ``summary_status = "..."`` (the DOMINANT cluster:
47:          L7918-7972, 882, 8235, 9115, ...) and ``summary["status"] = "..."``;
48:       b. direct ``<x>manifest["status"] = "..."`` subscript assignment;
49:       c. DICT-LITERAL construction — ``{"status": "...", ...}`` — however it is
50:          consumed: a Name-bound manifest dict (``budget_manifest =
51:          {"status": "abort_budget_exceeded", ...}`` → ``manifest.json``),
52:          ``manifest.update({"status": "..."})`` / ``abort_manifest.update(...)``,
53:          or an inline ``write_text(json.dumps({"status": "..."}))``. Caught by an
54:          ``ast.Dict``-with-``"status"``-key walk so the consumption form is
55:          irrelevant — the reference ``test_manifest_contract_abort_statuses_are
56:          _authoritative`` uses the same source-scan-minus-telemetry strategy.
57:
58:     Every such literal MUST be *registered* (see REGISTRATION below). This is
59:     what catches a NEW literal status written into the runner WITHOUT being added
60:     to the declared taxonomy — that literal would otherwise escape the
61:     declared-set parity check entirely (P1.2: a post-extraction set-union test
62:     would not bite on real source drift).
63:
64:  Sweep-level / event telemetry ``"status":`` literals that are NOT manifest
65:  producers are excluded by a TIGHTLY-SCOPED, documented carve-out (mirrors the
66:  reference test's exclusion list — NOT a broad allowlist). Each is provably never
67:  a run ``manifest.status``:
68:    * ``abort_quota_exceeded`` — written to ``sweep_quota_refusal.json`` (a
69:      SWEEP-level refusal artifact), never a per-run manifest;
70:    * ``not_applicable_planner_lane`` — FX-14 custody-lane honesty marker, written
71:      ONLY to ``custody_lane_status.json``;
72:    * ``started`` — the in-memory ``summary["status"]`` sentinel / run-start event
73:      payload, overwritten before every return, never persisted to a manifest.
74:  A NEW unrecognised dict-literal status is NOT on this list → it bites.
75:
76:REGISTRATION INVARIANT (what makes a literal "registered")
77:----------------------------------------------------------
78:``manifest.status`` is written either directly (a unified value) or via
79:``to_unified_status(summary_status)``. So:
80:
81:  * a ``summary`` / ``summary_status`` literal is registered iff it is a KEY of
82:    ``_SUMMARY_TO_UNIFIED`` (it gets mapped) OR already a member of
83:    ``UNIFIED_STATUS_VALUES`` (it is written into summary-space as a final unified
84:    value — e.g. ``summary["status"] = "cancelled"``, which is NOT a map key but
85:    IS a unified value);
86:  * a direct ``*manifest["status"]`` literal AND a dict-literal manifest
87:    ``"status"`` value are registered iff they are members of
88:    ``UNIFIED_STATUS_VALUES`` (they land in the manifest verbatim).
89:
90:An UNREGISTERED literal = a status the runner can write that the declared
91:taxonomy does not know = it would reach ``manifest.status`` (directly, or as the
92:``error_unexpected`` default of an unmapped ``summary_status``) and could escape
93:the downstream-parity check. The gate FAILS on it.
94:
95:ASSUMPTION: the three registries are defined as literal collections
96:(``frozenset({...})`` / ``{...}`` dict / ``Literal[...]`` / ``frozenset(dict)``).
97:If a future refactor builds one via a runtime union (e.g. ``frozenset({...}) |
98:{...}``) the literal extractor would under-read; the ``"success" in extracted``
99:sanity assert on each set guards the total-failure case, and the gate runs on
100:every change to these files so a shape change is caught at review time.

117:# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
118:# Pure parity logic — (runner_set, downstream_set) -> missing.
119:# Kept pure (no IO, no import side effects) so the injection tests can prove the
120:# gate bites WITHOUT touching the real runner file.
121:# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
122:def find_missing_statuses(
123:    runner_statuses: typing.Iterable[str],
124:    downstream_statuses: typing.Iterable[str],
125:) -> set[str]:
126:    """Return the runner statuses that are NOT present downstream.
127:
128:    An empty result means parity holds. A non-empty result is real drift = CI
129:    FAIL. There is NO whitelist/baseline: the registries are reconciled so parity
130:    is GENUINE, and any new drift surfaces immediately.
131:    """
132:    return set(runner_statuses) - set(downstream_statuses)

135:# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
136:# Static (AST) extraction helpers — no module import, pure source read.
137:# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
138:def _str_constants(node: ast.AST | None) -> set[str]:
139:    """All str-constant elements of a Set / List / Tuple literal node."""
140:    out: set[str] = set()
141:    if isinstance(node, (ast.Set, ast.List, ast.Tuple)):
142:        for elt in node.elts:
143:            if isinstance(elt, ast.Constant) and isinstance(elt.value, str):
144:                out.add(elt.value)
145:    return out
146:
147:
148:def _iter_named_assignments(tree: ast.AST):
149:    """Yield (target_name, value_node) for top-level/`AnnAssign`/`Assign` bindings
150:    to a single ``Name`` target."""
151:    for node in ast.walk(tree):
152:        if isinstance(node, ast.AnnAssign) and isinstance(node.target, ast.Name):
153:            yield node.target.id, node.value
154:        elif (
155:            isinstance(node, ast.Assign)
156:            and len(node.targets) == 1
157:            and isinstance(node.targets[0], ast.Name)
158:        ):
159:            yield node.targets[0].id, node.value
160:
161:
162:def _is_status_subscript(target: ast.AST) -> bool:
163:    """True for ``<name>["status"]`` where the base name is ``summary`` or ends in
164:    ``manifest`` (covers ``manifest``, ``_pm_manifest``, ``_ja_manifest``)."""
165:    if not isinstance(target, ast.Subscript) or not isinstance(target.value, ast.Name):
166:        return False
167:    base = target.value.id
168:    if not (base == "summary" or base == "manifest" or base.endswith("manifest")):
169:        return False
170:    sl = target.slice  # py3.9+: index node directly
171:    return isinstance(sl, ast.Constant) and sl.value == "status"
172:
173:
174:# Telemetry ``"status":`` dict-literals that are PROVABLY NOT a run manifest.status
175:# (mirrors the carve-out in tests/.../test_manifest_contract.py — tightly scoped,
176:# NOT a broad allowlist). A NEW unrecognised dict-literal status is not here → bites.
177:_TELEMETRY_STATUS_LITERALS: frozenset[str] = frozenset({
178:    "abort_quota_exceeded",          # sweep_quota_refusal.json — sweep-level, never a run manifest
179:    "not_applicable_planner_lane",   # custody_lane_status.json — FX-14 custody marker, never a manifest
180:    "started",                       # in-memory summary sentinel / run-start event — never persisted
181:})
182:
183:
184:def _scanned_status_emissions(runner_source: str) -> dict[str, set[str]]:
185:    """STATIC scan of the runner for the LITERAL statuses it emits into status-
186:    space, split by destination so the registration invariant can be applied:
187:
188:      * ``"summary"`` — literals written to ``summary["status"]`` or to a plain
189:        ``summary_status`` Name (the dominant cluster: L7918-7972, 882, 8235, ...).
190:        These are mapped through ``to_unified_status`` (or already unified), so the
191:        registration check allows ``_SUMMARY_TO_UNIFIED`` keys ∪ UNIFIED.
192:      * ``"manifest"`` — literals that land in the manifest VERBATIM, via either
193:        (a) a direct ``<x>manifest["status"]`` subscript assignment, OR
194:        (b) a DICT-LITERAL ``{"status": "...", ...}`` (a Name-bound manifest dict,
195:            ``manifest.update({...})`` / ``abort_manifest.update({...})``, or an
196:            inline ``write_text(json.dumps({...}))``). These must be UNIFIED members.
197:
198:    The dict-literal form is recovered by an ``ast.Dict``-with-``"status"``-key walk
199:    so the consumption form (assignment / ``.update()`` / ``json.dumps`` arg) does
200:    not matter. Provable telemetry literals (``_TELEMETRY_STATUS_LITERALS``) are
201:    excluded — they are written only to sweep/custody/event artifacts, never to a
202:    run ``manifest.json``.
203:    """
204:    tree = ast.parse(runner_source)
205:    summary_literals: set[str] = set()
206:    manifest_literals: set[str] = set()
207:
208:    for node in ast.walk(tree):
209:        # Form (a)/(summary): str-Constant assigned to a status-space target.
210:        if isinstance(node, ast.Assign):
211:            value = node.value
212:            if isinstance(value, ast.Constant) and isinstance(value.value, str):
213:                literal = value.value
214:                for target in node.targets:
215:                    # Plain Name: ``summary_status = "..."`` (dominant cluster).
216:                    if isinstance(target, ast.Name) and target.id == "summary_status":
217:                        summary_literals.add(literal)
218:                    # Subscript: ``summary["status"] = "..."`` / ``*manifest["status"] = "..."``.
219:                    elif _is_status_subscript(target):
220:                        base = target.value.id  # type: ignore[union-attr]

242:
243:def _extract_runner_declared_taxonomy(runner_source: str) -> dict[str, set[str]]:
244:    """Parse the runner's DECLARED status registries:
245:
246:      * ``UNIFIED_STATUS_VALUES`` (a ``frozenset({...})`` annotated assign),
247:      * ``_SUMMARY_TO_UNIFIED`` (a dict) — both its KEYS (legacy labels accepted by
248:        ``to_unified_status``) and VALUES (what those map to).
249:
250:    Returns ``{"unified", "summary_keys", "summary_values"}``.
251:    """
252:    tree = ast.parse(runner_source)
253:    unified: set[str] = set()
254:    summary_keys: set[str] = set()
255:    summary_values: set[str] = set()
256:
257:    for name, value in _iter_named_assignments(tree):
258:        if value is None:
259:            continue
260:        if name == "UNIFIED_STATUS_VALUES" and isinstance(value, ast.Call):
261:            # frozenset({ "a", "b", ... }) — the set literal is the sole arg.
262:            if value.args:
263:                unified |= _str_constants(value.args[0])
264:        if name == "_SUMMARY_TO_UNIFIED" and isinstance(value, ast.Dict):
265:            for k in value.keys:
266:                if isinstance(k, ast.Constant) and isinstance(k.value, str):
267:                    summary_keys.add(k.value)
268:            for v in value.values:
269:                if isinstance(v, ast.Constant) and isinstance(v.value, str):
270:                    summary_values.add(v.value)
271:
272:    return {"unified": unified, "summary_keys": summary_keys, "summary_values": summary_values}
273:
274:
275:def _extract_runner_status_producers(runner_source: str) -> set[str]:
276:    """The set of strings that can land in ``manifest.status`` (the DECLARED
277:    producer set): ``UNIFIED_STATUS_VALUES`` ∪ ``_SUMMARY_TO_UNIFIED`` values."""
278:    declared = _extract_runner_declared_taxonomy(runner_source)
279:    return declared["unified"] | declared["summary_values"]
280:
281:
282:def _find_unregistered_emissions(runner_source: str) -> set[str]:
283:    """STATIC drift detector: every literal status the runner EMITS into status-
284:    space must be REGISTERED in the declared taxonomy. Returns the unregistered
285:    literals (empty == every emission is registered).
286:
287:    Registration (per the docstring invariant):
288:      * a ``summary`` literal ∈ (_SUMMARY_TO_UNIFIED keys ∪ UNIFIED_STATUS_VALUES);
289:      * a direct ``manifest`` literal ∈ UNIFIED_STATUS_VALUES.
290:    """
291:    declared = _extract_runner_declared_taxonomy(runner_source)
292:    unified = declared["unified"]
293:    summary_registered = declared["summary_keys"] | unified
294:
295:    emissions = _scanned_status_emissions(runner_source)
296:    bad: set[str] = set()
297:    bad |= {s for s in emissions["summary"] if s not in summary_registered}
298:    bad |= {s for s in emissions["manifest"] if s not in unified}
299:    return bad
300:
301:
302:def _extract_pipeline_status_literal(run_status_source: str) -> set[str]:
303:    """Parse the ``PipelineStatus = Literal["a", "b", ...]`` assignment — a
304:    ``Subscript`` whose slice is a Tuple of str Constants."""
305:    tree = ast.parse(run_status_source)
306:    for name, value in _iter_named_assignments(tree):
307:        if name != "PipelineStatus" or not isinstance(value, ast.Subscript):
308:            continue
309:        sl = value.slice  # py3.9+: the index node directly
310:        if isinstance(sl, (ast.Tuple, ast.List, ast.Set)):
311:            return _str_constants(sl)
312:        if isinstance(sl, ast.Constant) and isinstance(sl.value, str):
313:            return {sl.value}  # single-element Literal
314:    return set()

317:def _extract_known_status_values(regression_lab_source: str) -> set[str]:
318:    """Parse ``KNOWN_STATUS_VALUES = frozenset(_STATUS_TIERS)`` by reading the KEYS
319:    of the ``_STATUS_TIERS`` dict literal it is derived from."""
320:    tree = ast.parse(regression_lab_source)
321:    status_tiers_keys: set[str] = set()
322:    for name, value in _iter_named_assignments(tree):
323:        if name == "_STATUS_TIERS" and isinstance(value, ast.Dict):
324:            for k in value.keys:
325:                if isinstance(k, ast.Constant) and isinstance(k.value, str):
326:                    status_tiers_keys.add(k.value)
327:    return status_tiers_keys

400:def test_every_runner_status_emission_site_is_registered():
401:    """P1.2: STATIC scan of the runner's ACTUAL literal emission sites
402:    (``summary["status"]`` / ``summary_status`` / ``*manifest["status"]``). Every
403:    emitted literal MUST be registered in the declared taxonomy — otherwise a new
404:    literal status written into the runner WITHOUT being added to
405:    UNIFIED_STATUS_VALUES / _SUMMARY_TO_UNIFIED would escape the parity gate (it

408:    assert not unregistered, (

410:        f"{sorted(unregistered)}. Add each summary literal as a _SUMMARY_TO_UNIFIED "
411:        "key (or a UNIFIED_STATUS_VALUES member if written as a final unified value), "
412:        "and each direct manifest literal to UNIFIED_STATUS_VALUES — otherwise it "
413:        "escapes the downstream status-schema parity gate."
414:    )

421:def test_gate_bites_on_injected_fake_downstream_drift():
422:    """Inject a fake status into the runner producer set and assert the parity
423:    function flags it against BOTH downstream registries. Proves the downstream
424:    parity check is not a tautology and that real parity holds today (the fake is
425:    the ONLY thing flagged — every real producer is genuinely present
426:    downstream, with no whitelist absorbing anything)."""

430:    missing_ps = find_missing_statuses(runner, _pipeline_status_values())
431:    assert missing_ps == {fake}, (
432:        f"expected ONLY the injected fake missing vs PipelineStatus, got {sorted(missing_ps)} "
433:        "— a non-empty residual means real (un-whitelisted) drift still exists."
434:    )

436:    missing_kn = find_missing_statuses(runner, _known_status_values())
437:    assert missing_kn == {fake}, (
438:        f"expected ONLY the injected fake missing vs KNOWN_STATUS_VALUES, got "
439:        f"{sorted(missing_kn)} — real drift still exists."
440:    )
